INTRODUCTION.

The following pages embody the text of a Sanskrit work on ‘doс╣гa’ (poetical blemishes) by one Gang─Бnanda Kavlndra,an inhabitant of Tirabhukta or Mithil─Б. It is the only Sanskrit work, so far known, devoted exclusively to an exposition of this topic.

The work is divided into five chapters, each called by the name of ‘Drс╣гti’. The first chapter deals with the definition of ‘doс╣гa’ and its classification. The definition of the ‘verbal faults’ (3*5193) 1) has been examined and illustrated. The remainig chapters treat respectively, in a similar manner, of the faults of aspects of WOK’S, of sentences, of meanings and of rasa. In the last chapter there appears also a discussion as to when a doс╣гa is regarded as a guс╣Зa, when its does not involve any defect at all, or when it is neutral so that it can not be treated either as a guс╣Зa or as a doс╣гa.

The author, whose name appers as Gang─Бnanda in the colophon,was a Maithil Brahman,beingthe younger brother of one Raghunatha to whom he refers (p. 37). Nothing is known about his parentage. He was a protege of Mah─Бr─Бja Karс╣Зa of Bikaner. The reign of Karс╣Зa-Sri Lui Karс╣Зa Deva-,son of Mahar─Бja Bik─Бji is generally assigned to 1506-1527 A. D. Hence Gang─Бnanda may be rightly placed in the beginning of the 16th century.

Apart from the work, herewith published, the following works are also attributed to the same author:

(1) Karс╣Зabh┼лsaс╣Зa1 (on Ram),
(2) Bhrngaduta2 (a poem), and
(3) Mandaraman^(v)jari3 (a drama).

The present edition of Kavyadakin─л is based on a single Ms., belonging originally to P. Mukunda S’─Бstri and now obtained for the Government Sanskrit Library, Sarasvati Bhavana, Benares. Leaves, 1-29. Size, 9-6^(n) x 3.6” inches. Lines 10 in a page, and letters 40 in a line. Material, country-made paper. Script, N─Бgari, Date, Saс╣Гvat 1748 (=1691 A.D). Transcribed by Mah─Бdeva (Puntamkar).Generally correct. The colophon at the end of the Ms runs thus: рд╡рд╕реБ рд╢реНрд░реАрдЬрдирд┐рджреНрд╡реАрдкрднреВрдорд┐рдорд┐рддреЗрдмреНрджреЗрезренрекрео рджреНрд╡рд┐рддреАрдпрд╛ рджрд┐рдиреЗ рдкреМрд╖ рдорд╛рд╕рд╕реНрдп рдХреГрд╖реНрдгреЗредрд╢реБрднреЗ рдорд╛рдереБрд░реЗрдордгреНрдбрд▓реЗ рд░рдореНрдпрд▓реЛрдХ рдорд╣рд╛рджреЗрд╡рдирд╛рдорд╛рд╜рд▓рд┐рдЦрджреН рдЧреНрд░рдиреНрдердореЗрддрдореНред рд╢реНрд░реАрдорд╣рд╛рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзреЗрд╢реНрд╡рд░реНрдпреНрдпреИрдирдордГред

Sarasvati Bhavan Library,
Benares. J a g
March 31, 1924.

Jagannath Sastri Hoshing
